std::io::Result<()> {\n375\t    let mut stdout = std::io::stdout();\n376\t\n377\t    // Disable raw mode first\n378\t    let _ = crossterm::terminal::disable_raw_mode();\n379\t\n380\t    // Leave crossterm::event::DisableMouseCapture\n385\t    )?;\n386\t\n387\t    // Show cursor\n388\t    crossterm::execute!(stdout, crossterm::cursor::Show)?;\n389\t\n390\t    // Flush to ensure all escape sequences are written\n391\t    stdout.flush()?;\n392\t\n393\t    Ok(())\n394\t}\n395\t\n396\t/// Set up logging based on CLI arguments.\n397\tfn setup_logging(cli: &Cli) -> forge_core::Result<LogGuard> {\n398\t    // Initialize logging with the specified log directory\n399\t    // Either --debug or -v/--verbose enables debug logging\n400\t    let debug = cli.debug || cli.verbose > 0;\n401\t    init_logging(cli.log_dir.clone(), debug)\n402\t}\n403\t\n404\t/// Check if onboarding is needed (no config.yaml exists).\n405\tfn needs_onboarding() -> bool {\n406\t    let forge_dir = get_forge_dir();\n407\t    let config_path = forge_dir.join(\"config.yaml\");\n408\t    !config_path.exists()\n409\t}\n410\t\n411\t/// Get the FORGE directory path (~/.forge).\n412\tfn get_forge_dir() -> std::path::PathBuf {\n413\t    dirs::home_dir()\n414\t        .expect(\"Could not determine home directory\")\n415\t        .join(\".forge\")\n416\t}\n417\t\n418\t/// Run the onboarding flow.\n419\t///\n420\t/// # Arguments\n421\t///\n422\t/// * `non_interactive` - If true, suppress output and auto-select backend\n423\t/// * `preferred_backend` - Optional backend to use (from FORGE_CHAT_BACKEND env var)\n424\tfn run_onboarding(\n425\t    non_interactive: bool,\n426\t    preferred_backend: Option<&str>,\n427\t) -> Result<(), Box<dyn std::error::Error>> {\n428\t    info!(\n429\t        \"Starting onboarding flow (non_interactive={}, preferred_backend={:?})\",\n430\t        non_interactive, preferred_backend\n431\t    );\n432\t\n433\t    // Detect CLI tools with diagnostics\n434\t    if !non_interactive {\n435\t        eprintln!(\"🔍 Detecting available CLI tools...\");\n436\t    }\n437\t    let (tools, diagnostics) = detection::detect_cli_tools_with_diagnostics()?;\n438\t\n439\t    // Filter to only show tools that are ready to use\n440\t    let ready_tools: Vec<_> = tools.iter().filter(|t| t.is_ready()).collect();\n441\t\n442\t    if ready_tools.is_empty() {\n443\t        // Use the guidance module to show detailed instructions (both interactive and non-interactive)\n444\t        eprint!(\"{}\", guidance::generate_guidance(Some(&diagnostics)));\n445\t        return Err(\"No compatible CLI tools available\".into());\n446\t    }\n447\t\n448\t    // Select the backend to use\n449\t    let selected_tool: detection::CliToolDetection = if let Some(backend) = preferred_backend {\n450\t        // Try to find the specified backend\n451\t        let normalized_backend = normalize_backend_name(backend);\n452\t        let found = tools.iter().find(|t| {\n453\t            let tool_name = normalize_backend_name(&t.name);\n454\t            tool_name == normalized_backend\n455\t        });\n456\t\n457\t        match found {\n458\t            Some(tool) => {\n459\t                if !tool.is_ready() {\n460\t                    eprintln!(\n461\t                        \"error: Backend '{}' is not ready: {}\",\n462\t                        backend,\n463\t                        tool.status_message()\n464\t                    );\n465\t                    if tool.status == detection::ToolStatus::MissingApiKey\n466\t                        && let Some(env_var) = &tool.api_key_env_var\n467\t                    {\n468\t                        eprintln!(\"Set the {} environment variable and try again\", env_var);\n469\t                    }\n470\t                    return Err(format!(\"Backend '{}' is not ready\", backend).into());\n471\t                }\n472\t                tool.clone()\n473\t            }\n474\t            None => {\n475\t                eprintln!(\"error: Backend '{}' not found\", backend);\n476\t                eprintln!(\n477\t                    \"Available backends: {}\",\n478\t                    tools\n479\t                        .iter()\n480\t                        .map(|t| t.name.as_str())\n481\t                        .collect::<Vec<_>>()\n482\t                        .join(\", \")\n483\t                );\n484\t                return Err(format!(\"Backend '{}' not found\", backend).into());\n485\t            }\n486\t        }\n487\t    } else if non_interactive {\n488\t        // Auto-select the first ready tool in non-interactive mode\n489\t        match tools.iter().find(|t| t.is_ready()) {\n490\t            Some(tool) => tool.clone(),\n491\t            None => {\n492\t                // Tools exist but none are ready - show specific guidance\n493\t                let not_ready: Vec<_> = tools\n494\t                    .iter()\n495\t                    .filter(|t| !t.is_ready())\n496\t                    .map(|t| {\n497\t                        let (missing_api_key, incompatible_version, missing_feature) = match t.status {\n498\t                            detection::ToolStatus::MissingApiKey => (true, false, None),\n499\t                            detection::ToolStatus::IncompatibleVersion => {\n500\t                                // Extract missing feature from diagnostics\n501\t                                let feature = diagnostics\n502\t                                    .rejections\n503\t                                    .iter()\n504\t                                    .find(|r| r.tool_name == t.name || r.tool_name == t.name.replace(\"-code\", \"\"))\n505\t                                    .and_then(|r| match &r.reason {\n506\t                                        guidance::RejectionReason::IncompatibleVersion { missing_feature, .. } => {\n507\t                                            Some(missing_feature.clone())\n508\t                                        }\n509\t                                        _ => None,\n510\t                                    });\n511\t                                (false, true, feature)\n512\t                            }\n513\t                            _ => (false, false, None),\n514\t                        };\n515\t                        guidance::ToolFixInfo {\n516\t                            name: t.name.clone(),\n517\t                            version: t.version.clone(),\n518\t                            missing_api_key,\n519\t                            api_key_env_var: t.api_key_env_var.clone(),\n520\t                            incompatible_version,\n521\t                            missing_feature,\n522\t                        }\n523\t                    })\n524\t                    .collect();\n525\t\n526\t                if !not_ready.is_empty() {\n527\t                    eprint!(\"{}\", guidance::generate_not_ready_guidance(&not_ready));\n528\t                }\n529\t                return Err(\"No ready tools available\".into());\n530\t            }\n531\t        }\n532\t    } else {\n533\t        // Interactive mode: show the TUI wizard for selection\n534\t        match wizard::run_wizard(tools.clone()) {\n535\t            Ok(Some(tool)) => {\n536\t                // User selected a tool\n537\t                eprintln!(\n538\t                    \"\\n✨ Using: {} ({})\",\n539\t                    tool.name,\n540\t                    tool.binary_path.display()\n541\t                );\n542\t                tool\n543\t            }\n544\t            Ok(None) => {\n545\t                // User chose \"Manual Setup\" - skip auto-configuration\n546\t                eprintln!(\"\\n📝 Manual setup selected.\");\n547\t                eprintln!(\"   Create ~/.forge/config.yaml manually to configure FORGE.\");\n548\t                return Ok(());\n549\t            }\n550\t            Err(wizard::WizardError::UserCancelled) => {\n551\t                eprintln!(\"\\n👋 Setup cancelled.\");\n552\t                return Err(\"User cancelled setup\".into());\n553\t            }\n554\t            Err(wizard::WizardError::NoToolsAvailable) => {\n555\t                // This shouldn't happen since we already checked, but handle it\n556\t                eprint!(\"{}\", guidance::generate_guidance(Some(&diagnostics)));\n557\t                return Err(\"No compatible CLI tools available\".into());\n558\t            }\n559\t            Err(e) => {\n560\t                eprintln!(\"\\nerror: Wizard failed: {}\", e);\n561\t                return Err(format!(\"Wizard failed: {}\", e).into());\n562\t            }\n563\t        }\n564\t    };\n565\t\n566\t    if non_interactive {\n567\t        // Only print in non-interactive mode (wizard already prints in interactive mode)\n568\t        info!(\n569\t            \"Auto-selected: {} ({})\",\n570\t            selected_tool.name,\n571\t            selected_tool.binary_path.display()\n572\t        );\n573\t    }\n574\t\n575\t    // Create directory structure\n576\t    let forge_dir = get_forge_dir();\n577\t    if !non_interactive {\n578\t        eprintln!(\"\\n📁 Creating directory structure...\");\n579\t    }\n580\t    generator::create_directory_structure(&forge_dir)?;\n581\t\n582\t    // Generate config.yaml\n583\t    let config_path = forge_dir.join(\"config.yaml\");\n584\t    if !non_interactive {\n585\t        eprintln!(\"📝 Generating config.yaml...\");\n586\t    }\n587\t    generator::generate_config_yaml(&selected_tool, &config_path)?;\n588\t\n589\t    // Generate launcher script\n590\t    let launcher_name = format!(\"{}-launcher\", selected_tool.name);\n591\t    let launcher_path = forge_dir.join(\"launchers\").join(&launcher_name);\n592\t    if !non_interactive {\n593\t        eprintln!(\"🚀 Generating launcher script...\");\n594\t    }\n595\t    generator::generate_launcher_script(&selected_tool, &launcher_path)?;\n596\t\n597\t    if !non_interactive {\n598\t        eprintln!(\"\\n✅ Configuration complete!\");\n599\t        eprintln!(\"   Config: {}\", config_path.display());\n600\t        eprintln!(\"   Launcher: {}\", launcher_path.display());\n601\t    }\n602\t\n603\t    info!(\n604\t        \"Onboarding complete: using {} backend\",\n605\t        selected_tool.name\n606\t    );\n607\t    Ok(())\n608\t}\n609\t\n610\t/// Normalize backend name for comparison.\n611\t///\n612\t/// Maps common aliases to canonical names:\n613\t/// - \"claude\", \"claude-code\", \"claudecode\" -> \"claude-code\"\n614\t/// - \"opencode\" -> \"opencode\"\n615\t/// - \"aider\" -> \"aider\"\n616\tfn normalize_backend_name(name: &str) -> String {\n617\t    let lower = name.to_lowercase();\n618\t    match lower.as_str() {\n619\t        \"claude\" | \"claude-code\" | \"claudecode\" => \"claude-code\".to_string(),\n620\t        other => other.to_string(),\n621\t    }\n622\t}\n623\t\n624\t/// Handle the `forge init` command.\n625\tfn handle_init_command(non_interactive: bool, force: bool, reconfigure: bool, detect_tools: bool) -> ExitCode {\n626\t    info!(\n627\t        \"Handling init command (non_interactive={}, force={}, reconfigure={}, detect_tools={})\",\n628\t        non_interactive, force, reconfigure, detect_tools\n629\t    );\n630\t\n631\t    // Handle --detect-tools: dry run that only shows detection results\n632\t    if detect_tools {\n633\t        return handle_detect_tools_command();\n634\t    }\n635\t\n636\t    let forge_dir = get_forge_dir();\n637\t    let config_path = forge_dir.join(\"config.yaml\");\n638\t\n639\t    // Handle --reconfigure: backup existing config before re-running setup\n640\t    if reconfigure {\n641\t        if !config_path.exists() {\n642\t            if non_interactive {\n643\t                eprintln!(\"error: No configuration found to reconfigure\");\n644\t                eprintln!(\"Use 'forge init' to create initial configuration\");\n645\t            } else {\n646\t                eprintln!(\"No configuration found. Running first-time setup instead...\\n\");\n647\t            }\n648\t            // Fall through to normal setup since there's nothing to reconfigure\n649\t        } else {\n650\t            // Backup existing config before proceeding\n651\t            if let Err(e) = backup_config(&forge_dir, &config_path) {\n652\t                eprintln!(\"❌ Failed to backup config: {}\", e);\n653\t                return ExitCode::from(1);\n654\t            }\n655\t            if !non_interactive {\n656\t                eprintln!(\"📦 Existing configuration backed up\\n\");\n657\t            }\n658\t        }\n659\t    } else if !force && config_path.exists() {\n660\t        // Neither --force nor --reconfigure: don't overwrite existing config\n661\t        if non_interactive {\n662\t            eprintln!(\n663\t                \"error: Configuration already exists at {}\",\n664\t                config_path.display()\n665\t            );\n666\t            eprintln!(\"Use --force to overwrite existing configuration\");\n667\t            eprintln!(\"Use --reconfigure to backup and re-run setup\");\n668\t            return ExitCode::from(1);\n669\t        } else {\n670\t            eprintln!(\n671\t                \"Configuration already exists at {}\",\n672\t                config_path.display()\n673\t            );\n674\t            eprintln!(\"Use --force to overwrite existing configuration\");\n675\t            eprintln!(\"Use --reconfigure to backup and re-run setup\");\n676\t            return ExitCode::SUCCESS;\n677\t        }\n678\t    }\n679\t\n680\t    // Get preferred backend from environment variable\n681\t    let preferred_backend = std::env::var(\"FORGE_CHAT_BACKEND\").ok();\n682\t\n683\t    if non_interactive {\n684\t        // Non-interactive mode: quiet output, clear error messages to stderr\n685\t        match run_onboarding(true, preferred_backend.as_deref()) {\n686\t            Ok(()) => ExitCode::SUCCESS,\n687\t            Err(_) => ExitCode::from(1),\n688\t        }\n689\t    } else {\n690\t        // Interactive mode: show welcome message and full output\n691\t        eprintln!(\"🚀 FORGE Setup\");\n692\t        eprintln!();\n693\t\n694\t        match run_onboarding(false, preferred_backend.as_deref()) {\n695\t            Ok(()) => {\n696\t                eprintln!(\"\\n✅ Setup complete!\");\n697\t                ExitCode::SUCCESS\n698\t            }\n699\t            Err(e) => {\n700\t                eprintln!(\"❌ Setup failed: {}\", e);\n701\t                ExitCode::from(1)\n702\t            }\n703\t        }\n704\t    }\n705\t}\n706\t\n707\t/// Backup existing config.yaml before reconfiguration.\n708\t///\n709\t/// Creates a timestamped backup to preserve user's previous settings.\n710\t/// Keeps logs, costs database, and status files intact.\n711\tfn backup_config(forge_dir: &std::path::Path, config_path: &std::path::Path) -> Result<std::path::PathBuf, Box<dyn std::error::Error>> {\n712\t    let timestamp = chrono::Local::now().format(\"%Y%m%d_%H%M%S\");\n713\t    let backup_path = forge_dir.join(format!(\"config.yaml.backup.{}\", timestamp));\n714\t\n715\t    std::fs::copy(config_path, &backup_path)?;\n716\t    info!(\"Backed up config to: {}\", backup_path.display());\n717\t\n718\t    // Check for launcher scripts that might have custom modifications\n719\t    let launchers_dir = forge_dir.join(\"launchers\");\n720\t    if launchers_dir.exists()\n721\t        && let Ok(entries) = std::fs::read_dir(&launchers_dir)\n722\t    {\n723\t        for entry in entries.flatten() {\n724\t            let path = entry.path();\n725\t            if path.is_file() {\n726\t                // Check if the file contains any comments that suggest custom modifications\n727\t                if let Ok(content) = std::fs::read_to_string(&path)\n728\t                    && (content.contains(\"# CUSTOM:\") || content.contains(\"# USER:\") || content.contains(\"# Modified by\")) {\n729\t                        eprintln!(\"⚠️  Warning: {} may contain custom modifications\", path.display());\n730\t                        // Backup the launcher script too\n731\t                        let launcher_backup = forge_dir.join(format!(\n732\t                            \"launchers/{}.backup.{}\",\n733\t                            entry.file_name().to_string_lossy(),\n734\t                            timestamp\n735\t                        ));\n736\t                        let _ = std::fs::copy(&path, &launcher_backup);\n737\t                    }\n738\t            }\n739\t        }\n740\t    }\n741\t\n742\t    Ok(backup_path)\n743\t}\n744\t\n745\t/// Handle the `forge init --detect-tools` command.\n746\t///\n747\t/// Runs CLI tool detection and displays results without modifying any files.\n748\tfn handle_detect_tools_command() -> ExitCode {\n749\t    info!(\"Running CLI tool detection (dry run)\");\n750\t\n751\t    eprintln!(\"🔍 Detecting available CLI tools...\\n\");\n752\t\n753\t    match detection::detect_cli_tools_with_diagnostics() {\n754\t        Ok((tools, diagnostics)) => {\n755\t            // Display all detected tools\n756\t            if tools.is_empty() {\n757\t                eprintln!(\"No CLI tools found.\\n\");\n758\t            } else {\n759\t                eprintln!(\"Detected CLI tools:\\n\");\n760\t                for tool in &tools {\n761\t                    let status_icon = match tool.status {\n762\t                        detection::ToolStatus::Ready => \"✅\",\n763\t                        detection::ToolStatus::MissingApiKey => \"⚠️ \",\n764\t                        detection::ToolStatus::IncompatibleVersion => \"❌\",\n765\t                        detection::ToolStatus::NotExecutable => \"❌\",\n766\t                    };\n767\t\n768\t                    eprintln!(\"  {} {} ({})\", status_icon, tool.name, tool.status_message());\n769\t                    eprintln!(\"      Path: {}\", tool.binary_path.display());\n770\t                    if let Some(version) = &tool.version {\n771\t                        eprintln!(\"      Version: {}\", version);\n772\t                    }\n773\t                    eprintln!(\"      Headless: {} | Skip-Perms: {}\",\n774\t                        if tool.headless_support { \"yes\" } else { \"no\" },\n775\t                        if tool.skip_permissions { \"yes\" } else { \"no\" }\n776\t                    );\n777\t                    if tool.api_key_required {\n778\t                        let key_status = if tool.api_key_detected { \"✅ found\" } else { \"❌ missing\" };\n779\t                        if let Some(env_var) = &tool.api_key_env_var {\n780\t                            eprintln!(\"      API Key: {} ({})\", key_status, env_var);\n781\t                        } else {\n782\t                            eprintln!(\"      API Key: {}\", key_status);\n783\t                        }\n784\t                    }\n785\t                    eprintln!();\n786\t                }\n787\t            }\n788\t\n789\t            // Display diagnostics about rejected/not-found tools\n790\t            if !diagnostics.rejections.is_empty() {\n791\t                eprintln!(\"Detection details:\");\n792\t                for rejection in &diagnostics.rejections {\n793\t                    match &rejection.reason {\n794\t                        guidance::RejectionReason::NotFound => {\n795\t                            eprintln!(\"  • {} - not found in PATH\", rejection.tool_name);\n796\t                        }\n797\t                        guidance::RejectionReason::MissingApiKey { env_var, .. } => {\n798\t                            eprintln!(\"  • {} - missing API key ({})\", rejection.tool_name, env_var);\n799\t                        }\n800\t                        guidance::RejectionReason::IncompatibleVersion { version, missing_feature, .. } => {\n801\t                            let ver = version.as_deref().unwrap_or(\"unknown\");\n802\t                            eprintln!(\"  • {} {} - incompatible: {}\", rejection.tool_name, ver, missing_feature);\n803\t                        }\n804\t                        guidance::RejectionReason::NotExecutable(_) => {\n805\t                            eprintln!(\"  • {} - not executable\", rejection.tool_name);\n806\t                        }\n807\t                    }\n808\t                }\n809\t                eprintln!();\n810\t            }\n811\t\n812\t            // Summary\n813\t            let ready_count = tools.iter().filter(|t| t.is_ready()).count();\n814\t            if ready_count > 0 {\n815\t                eprintln!(\"✅ {} tool(s) ready for use\", ready_count);\n816\t                eprintln!(\"   Run 'forge init' to configure\");\n817\t            } else {\n818\t                eprintln!(\"❌ No compatible tools ready\");\n819\t                eprintln!(\"   Install Claude Code, OpenCode, or configure API keys\");\n820\t            }\n821\t\n822\t            ExitCode::SUCCESS\n823\t        }\n824\t        Err(e) => {\n825\t            eprintln!(\"❌ Detection failed: {}\", e);\n826\t            ExitCode::from(1)\n827\t        }\n828\t    }\n829\t}\n830\t\n831\t/// Validate the config file and offer recovery if invalid.\n832\tfn validate_config() -> Result<(), String> {\n833\t    use std::io::{self, Write};\n834\t\n835\t    match ForgeConfig::load_with_error() {\n836\t        Ok(_config) => {\n837\t            info!(\"Configuration validated successfully\");\n838\t            Ok(())\n839\t        }\n840\t        Err(e) => {\n841\t            // Format the error with line/column information\n842\t            eprintln!(\"❌ Configuration Error\");\n843\t            eprintln!();\n844\t\n845\t            let path_str = e.path().map(|p| p.display().to_string())\n846\t                .unwrap_or_else(|| \"~/.forge/config.yaml\".to_string());\n847\t\n848\t            if let (Some(line), Some(col)) = (e.line_number(), e.column_number()) {\n849\t                eprintln!(\"  File: {}\", path_str);\n850\t                eprintln!(\"  Line: {}, Column: {}\", line, col);\n851\t                eprintln!(\"  Error: {}\", e);\n852\t            } else {\n853\t                eprintln!(\"  {}\", e);\n854\t            }\n855\t            eprintln!();\n856\t\n857\t            // Offer recovery options\n858\t            eprintln!(\"Recovery options:\");\n859\t            eprintln!(\"  1) Reset to default configuration (creates backup)\");\n860\t            eprintln!(\"  2) Use defaults without modifying file (temporary)\");\n861\t            eprintln!(\"  3) Exit and fix manually\");\n862\t            eprintln!();\n863\t            eprint!(\"Choose option [1-3]: \");\n864\t            io::stdout().flush().map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;\n865\t\n866\t            let mut choice = String::new();\n867\t            io::stdin().read_line(&mut choice).map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;\n868\t\n869\t            match choice.trim() {\n870\t                \"1\" => {\n871\t                    if let Err(e) = reset_config_to_defaults() {\n872\t                        return Err(format!(\"Failed to reset config: {}\", e));\n873\t                    }\n874\t                    eprintln!(\"✅ Configuration reset to defaults\");\n875\t                    eprintln!(\"   Previous config backed up\");\n876\t                    eprintln!();\n877\t                    Ok(())\n878\t                }\n879\t                \"2\" => {\n880\t                    eprintln!(\"⚠️  Using default configuration (file not modified)\");\n881\t                    eprintln!(\"   Fix the config file manually or delete it to regenerate\");\n882\t                    eprintln!();\n883\t                    Ok(())\n884\t                }\n885\t                \"3\" | \"\" => {\n886\t                    Err(\"Exiting. Please fix the config file and try again.\".to_string())\n887\t                }\n888\t                _ => {\n889\t                    Err(\"Invalid choice. Exiting.\".to_string())\n890\t                }\n891\t            }\n892\t        }\n893\t    }\n894\t}\n895\t\n896\t/// Reset config file to defaults with backup.\n897\tfn reset_config_to_defaults() -> Result<(), Box<dyn std::error::Error>> {\n898\t    let forge_dir = get_forge_dir();\n899\t    let config_path = forge_dir.join(\"config.yaml\");\n900\t\n901\t    // Create backup\n902\t    if timestamp));\n905\t        std::fs::copy(&config_path, &backup_path)?;\n906\t        info!(\"Created config backup: {}\", backup_path.display());\n907\t    }\n908\t\n909\t    // Generate default config\n910\t    let default_config = r#\"# FORGE Configuration\n911\t# This file was automatically generated after a config error.\n912\t\n913\tdashboard:\n914\t  refresh_interval_ms: 1000\n915\t cli.user.unwrap_or_else(|| \"viewer\".to_string()),\n            cli.password.unwrap_or_else(|| \"viewer123\".to_string()),\n        );\n    }\n\n    // Mark startup as successful (app initialized without crashing)\n    #[cfg(feature = \"self-update\")]\n    {\n        if let Err(e) = forge_core::mark_startup_successful() {\n            error!(\"Failed to mark startup as successful: {}\", e);\n            // Don't fail just because of this\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Log terminal dimensions for debugging\n    if let Ok((cols, rows)) = crossterm::terminal::size() {\n        info!(\"Terminal size: {}x{} (columns x rows)\", cols, rows);\n        eprintln!(\"Terminal size: {}x{} (columns x rows)\", cols, rows);\n    } else {\n        error!(\"Failed to get terminal size\");\n    }\n\n    // Run the TUI application\n    match run_app() {\n        Ok(()) => {\n            info!(\"FORGE dashboard exited normally\");\n            ExitCode::SUCCESS\n        }\n        Err(e) => {\n            error!(\"FORGE dashboard error: {}\", e);\n            eprintln!(\"Error: {}\", e);\n            ExitCode::from(1)\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Install a panic hook that restores the terminal before printing the panic message.\n///\n/// This ensures that even if the application panics while in raw mode with the\n/// alternate screen enabled, the terminal will be properly restored so the user\n/// can see the panic message and continue using their terminal.\nfn install_panic_hook() {\n    let original_hook = panic::take_hook();\n\n    panic::set_hook(Box::new(move |panic_info| {\n        // Attempt to restore terminal state\n        let _ = restore_terminal();\n\n        // Call the original panic hook to print the panic message\n        original_hook(panic_info);\n    }));\n}\n\n/// Restore terminal to its normal state.\n///\n/// This function is called both on normal exit and during panic handling.\nfn restore_terminal() -> std::io::Result<()> {\n    let mut stdout = std::io::stdout();\n\n    // Disable raw mode first\n    let _ = crossterm::terminal::disable_raw_mode();\n\n    // Leave alternate screen and disable mouse capture\n    crossterm::execute!(\n        stdout,\n        crossterm::terminal::LeaveAlternateScreen,\n        crossterm::event::DisableMouseCapture\n    )?;\n\n    // Show cursor\n    crossterm::execute!(stdout, crossterm::cursor::Show)?;\n\n    // Flush to ensure all escape sequences are written\n    stdout.flush()?;\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Set up logging based on CLI arguments.\nfn setup_logging(cli: &Cli) -> forge_core::Result<LogGuard> {\n    // Initialize logging with the specified log directory\n    // Either --debug or -v/--verbose enables debug logging\n    let debug = cli.debug || cli.verbose > 0;\n    init_logging(cli.log_dir.clone(), debug)\n}\n\n/// Check if onboarding is needed (no config.yaml exists).\nfn needs_onboarding() -> bool {\n    let forge_dir = get_forge_dir();\n    let config_path = forge_dir.join(\"config.yaml\");\n    !config_path.exists()\n}\n\n/// Get the FORGE directory path (~/.forge).\nfn get_forge_dir() -> std::path::PathBuf {\n    dirs::home_dir()\n        .expect(\"Could not determine home directory\")\n        .join(\".forge\")\n}\n\n/// Run the onboarding flow.\n///\n/// # Arguments\n///\n/// * `non_interactive` - If true, suppress output and auto-select backend\n/// * `preferred_backend` - Optional backend to use (from FORGE_CHAT_BACKEND env var)\nfn run_onboarding(\n    non_interactive: bool,\n    preferred_backend: Option<&str>,\n) -> Result<(), Box<dyn std::error::Error>> {\n    info!(\n        \"Starting onboarding flow (non_interactive={}, preferred_backend={:?})\",\n        non_interactive, preferred_backend\n    );\n\n    // Detect CLI tools with diagnostics\n    if !non_interactive {\n        eprintln!(\"🔍 Detecting available CLI tools...\");\n    }\n    let (tools, diagnostics) = detection::detect_cli_tools_with_diagnostics()?;\n\n    // Filter to only show tools that are ready to use\n    let ready_tools: Vec<_> = tools.iter().filter(|t| t.is_ready()).collect();\n\n    if ready_tools.is_empty() {\n        // Use the guidance module to show detailed instructions (both interactive and non-interactive)\n        eprint!(\"{}\", guidance::generate_guidance(Some(&diagnostics)));\n        return Err(\"No compatible CLI tools available\".into());\n    }\n\n    // Select the backend to use\n    let selected_tool: detection::CliToolDetection = if let Some(backend) = preferred_backend {\n        // Try to find the specified backend\n        let normalized_backend = normalize_backend_name(backend);\n        let found = tools.iter().find(|t| {\n            let tool_name = normalize_backend_name(&t.name);\n            tool_name == normalized_backend\n        });\n\n        match found {\n            Some(tool) => {\n                if !tool.is_ready() {\n                    eprintln!(\n                        \"error: Backend '{}' is not ready: {}\",\n                        backend,\n                        tool.status_message()\n                    );\n                    if tool.status == detection::ToolStatus::MissingApiKey\n                        && let Some(env_var) = &tool.api_key_env_var\n                    {\n                        eprintln!(\"Set the {} environment variable and try again\", env_var);\n                    }\n                    return Err(format!(\"Backend '{}' is not ready\", backend).into());\n                }\n                tool.clone()\n            }\n            None => {\n                eprintln!(\"error: Backend '{}' not found\", backend);\n                eprintln!(\n                    \"Available backends: {}\",\n                    tools\n                        .iter()\n                        .map(|t| t.name.as_str())\n                        .collect::<Vec<_>>()\n                        .join(\", \")\n                );\n                return Err(format!(\"Backend '{}' not found\", backend).into());\n            }\n        }\n    } else if non_interactive {\n        // Auto-select the first ready tool in non-interactive mode\n        match tools.iter().find(|t| t.is_ready()) {\n            Some(tool) => tool.clone(),\n            None => {\n                // Tools exist but none are ready - show specific guidance\n                let not_ready: Vec<_> = tools\n                    .iter()\n                    .filter(|t| !t.is_ready())\n                    .map(|t| {\n                        let (missing_api_key, incompatible_version, missing_feature) = match t.status {\n                            detection::ToolStatus::MissingApiKey => (true, false, None),\n                            detection::ToolStatus::IncompatibleVersion => {\n                                // Extract missing feature from diagnostics\n                                let feature = diagnostics\n                                    .rejections\n                                    .iter()\n                                    .find(|r| r.tool_name == t.name || r.tool_name == t.name.replace(\"-code\", \"\"))\n                                    .and_then(|r| match &r.reason {\n                                        guidance::RejectionReason::IncompatibleVersion { missing_feature, .. } => {\n                                            Some(missing_feature.clone())\n                                        }\n                                        _ => None,\n                                    });\n                                (false, true, feature)\n                            }\n                            _ => (false, false, None),\n                        };\n                        guidance::ToolFixInfo {\n                            name: t.name.clone(),\n                            version: t.version.clone(),\n                            missing_api_key,\n                            api_key_env_var: t.api_key_env_var.clone(),\n                            incompatible_version,\n                            missing_feature,\n                        }\n                    })\n                    .collect();\n\n                if !not_ready.is_empty() {\n                    eprint!(\"{}\", guidance::generate_not_ready_guidance(&not_ready));\n                }\n                return Err(\"No ready tools available\".into());\n            }\n        }\n    } else {\n        // Interactive mode: show the TUI wizard for selection\n        match wizard::run_wizard(tools.clone()) {\n            Ok(Some(tool)) => {\n                // User selected a tool\n                eprintln!(\n                    \"\\n✨ Using: {} ({})\",\n                    tool.name,\n                    tool.binary_path.display()\n                );\n                tool\n            }\n            Ok(None) => {\n                // User chose \"Manual Setup\" - skip auto-configuration\n                eprintln!(\"\\n📝 Manual setup selected.\");\n                eprintln!(\"   Create ~/.forge/config.yaml manually to configure FORGE.\");\n                return Ok(());\n            }\n            Err(wizard::WizardError::UserCancelled) => {\n                eprintln!(\"\\n👋 Setup cancelled.\");\n                return Err(\"User cancelled setup\".into());\n            }\n            Err(wizard::WizardError::NoToolsAvailable) => {\n                // This shouldn't happen since we already checked, but handle it\n                eprint!(\"{}\", guidance::generate_guidance(Some(&diagnostics)));\n                return Err(\"No compatible CLI tools available\".into());\n            }\n            Err(e) => {\n                eprintln!(\"\\nerror: Wizard failed: {}\", e);\n                return Err(format!(\"Wizard failed: {}\", e).into());\n            }\n        }\n    };\n\n    if non_interactive {\n        // Only print in non-interactive mode (wizard already prints in interactive mode)\n        info!(\n            \"Auto-selected: {} ({})\",\n            selected_tool.name,\n            selected_tool.binary_path.display()\n        );\n    }\n\n    // Create directory structure\n    let forge_dir = get_forge_dir();\n    if !non_interactive {\n        eprintln!(\"\\n📁 Creating directory structure...\");\n    }\n    generator::create_directory_structure(&forge_dir)?;\n\n    // Generate config.yaml\n    let config_path = forge_dir.join(\"config.yaml\");\n    if !non_interactive {\n        eprintln!(\"📝 Generating config.yaml...\");\n    }\n    generator::generate_config_yaml(&selected_tool, &config_path)?;\n\n    // Generate launcher script\n    let launcher_name = format!(\"{}-launcher\", selected_tool.name);\n    let launcher_path = forge_dir.join(\"launchers\").join(&launcher_name);\n    if !non_interactive {\n        eprintln!(\"🚀 Generating launcher script...\");\n    }\n    generator::generate_launcher_script(&selected_tool, &launcher_path)?;\n\n    if !non_interactive {\n        eprintln!(\"\\n✅ Configuration complete!\");\n        eprintln!(\"   Config: {}\", config_path.display());\n        eprintln!(\"   Launcher: {}\", launcher_path.display());\n    }\n\n    info!(\n        \"Onboarding complete: using {} backend\",\n        selected_tool.name\n    );\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Normalize backend name for comparison.\n///\n/// Maps common aliases to canonical names:\n/// - \"claude\", \"claude-code\", \"claudecode\" -> \"claude-code\"\n/// - \"opencode\" -> \"opencode\"\n/// - \"aider\" -> \"aider\"\nfn normalize_backend_name(name: &str) -> String {\n    let lower = name.to_lowercase();\n    match lower.as_str() {\n        \"claude\" | \"claude-code\" | \"claudecode\" => \"claude-code\".to_string(),\n        other => other.to_string(),\n    }\n}\n\n/// Handle the `forge init` command.\nfn handle_init_command(non_interactive: bool, force: bool, reconfigure: bool, detect_tools: bool) -> ExitCode {\n    info!(\n        \"Handling init command (non_interactive={}, force={}, reconfigure={}, detect_tools={})\",\n        non_interactive, force, reconfigure, detect_tools\n    );\n\n    // Handle --detect-tools: dry run that only shows detection results\n    if detect_tools {\n        return handle_detect_tools_command();\n    }\n\n    let forge_dir = get_forge_dir();\n    let config_path = forge_dir.join(\"config.yaml\");\n\n    // Handle --reconfigure: backup existing config before re-running setup\n    if reconfigure {\n        if !config_path.exists() {\n            if non_interactive {\n                eprintln!(\"error: No configuration found to reconfigure\");\n                eprintln!(\"Use 'forge init' to create initial configuration\");\n            } else {\n                eprintln!(\"No configuration found. Running first-time setup instead...\\n\");\n            }\n            // Fall through to normal setup since there's nothing to reconfigure\n        } else {\n            // Backup existing config before proceeding\n            if let Err(e) = backup_config(&forge_dir, &config_path) {\n                eprintln!(\"❌ Failed to backup config: {}\", e);\n                return ExitCode::from(1);\n            }\n            if !non_interactive {\n                eprintln!(\"📦 Existing configuration backed up\\n\");\n            }\n        }\n    } else if !force && config_path.exists() {\n        // Neither --force nor --reconfigure: don't overwrite existing config\n        if non_interactive {\n            eprintln!(\n                \"error: Configuration already exists at {}\",\n                config_path.display()\n            );\n            eprintln!(\"Use --force to overwrite existing configuration\");\n            eprintln!(\"Use --reconfigure to backup and re-run setup\");\n            return ExitCode::from(1);\n        } else {\n            eprintln!(\n                \"Configuration already exists at {}\",\n                config_path.display()\n            );\n            eprintln!(\"Use --force to overwrite existing configuration\");\n            eprintln!(\"Use --reconfigure to backup and re-run setup\");\n            return ExitCode::SUCCESS;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Get preferred backend from environment variable\n    let preferred_backend = std::env::var(\"FORGE_CHAT_BACKEND\").ok();\n\n    if non_interactive {\n        // Non-interactive mode: quiet output, clear error messages to stderr\n        match run_onboarding(true, preferred_backend.as_deref()) {\n            Ok(()) => ExitCode::SUCCESS,\n            Err(_) => ExitCode::from(1),\n        }\n    } else {\n        // Interactive mode: show welcome message and full output\n        eprintln!(\"🚀 FORGE Setup\");\n        eprintln!();\n\n        match run_onboarding(false, preferred_backend.as_deref()) {\n            Ok(()) => {\n                eprintln!(\"\\n✅ Setup complete!\");\n                ExitCode::SUCCESS\n            }\n            Err(e) => {\n                eprintln!(\"❌ Setup failed: {}\", e);\n                ExitCode::from(1)\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Backup existing config.yaml before reconfiguration.\n///\n/// Creates a timestamped backup to preserve user's previous settings.\n/// Keeps logs, costs database, and status files intact.\nfn backup_config(forge_dir: &std::path::Path, config_path: &std::path::Path) -> Result<std::path::PathBuf, Box<dyn std::error::Error>> {\n    let timestamp = chrono::Local::now().format(\"%Y%m%d_%H%M%S\");\n    let backup_path = forge_dir.join(format!(\"config.yaml.backup.{}\", timestamp));\n\n    std::fs::copy(config_path, &backup_path)?;\n    info!(\"Backed up config to: {}\", backup_path.display());\n\n    // Check for launcher scripts that might have custom modifications\n    let launchers_dir = forge_dir.join(\"launchers\");\n    if launchers_dir.exists()\n        && let Ok(entries) = std::fs::read_dir(&launchers_dir)\n    {\n        for entry in entries.flatten() {\n            let path = entry.path();\n            if path.is_file() {\n                // Check if the file contains any comments that suggest custom modifications\n                if let Ok(content) = std::fs::read_to_string(&path)\n                    && (content.contains(\"# CUSTOM:\") || content.contains(\"# USER:\") || content.contains(\"# Modified by\")) {\n                        eprintln!(\"⚠️  Warning: {} may contain custom modifications\", path.display());\n                        // Backup the launcher script too\n                        let launcher_backup = forge_dir.join(format!(\n                            \"launchers/{}.backup.{}\",\n                            entry.file_name().to_string_lossy(),\n                            timestamp\n                        ));\n                        let _ = std::fs::copy(&path, &launcher_backup);\n                    }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    Ok(backup_path)\n}\n\n/// Handle the `forge init --detect-tools` command.\n///\n/// Runs CLI tool detection and displays results without modifying any files.\nfn handle_detect_tools_command() -> ExitCode {\n    info!(\"Running CLI tool detection (dry run)\");\n\n    eprintln!(\"🔍 Detecting available CLI tools...\\n\");\n\n    match detection::detect_cli_tools_with_diagnostics() {\n        Ok((tools, diagnostics)) => {\n            // Display all detected tools\n            if tools.is_empty() {\n                eprintln!(\"No CLI tools found.\\n\");\n            } else {\n                eprintln!(\"Detected CLI tools:\\n\");\n                for tool in &tools {\n                    let status_icon = match tool.status {\n                        detection::ToolStatus::Ready => \"✅\",\n                        detection::ToolStatus::MissingApiKey => \"⚠️ \",\n                        detection::ToolStatus::IncompatibleVersion => \"❌\",\n                        detection::ToolStatus::NotExecutable => \"❌\",\n                    };\n\n                    eprintln!(\"  {} {} ({})\", status_icon, tool.name, tool.status_message());\n                    eprintln!(\"      Path: {}\", tool.binary_path.display());\n                    if let Some(version) = &tool.version {\n                        eprintln!(\"      Version: {}\", version);\n                    }\n                    eprintln!(\"      Headless: {} | Skip-Perms: {}\",\n                        if tool.headless_support { \"yes\" } else { \"no\" },\n                        if tool.skip_permissions { \"yes\" } else { \"no\" }\n                    );\n                    if tool.api_key_required {\n                        let key_status = if tool.api_key_detected { \"✅ found\" } else { \"❌ missing\" };\n                        if let Some(env_var) = &tool.api_key_env_var {\n                            eprintln!(\"      API Key: {} ({})\", key_status, env_var);\n                        } else {\n                            eprintln!(\"      API Key: {}\", key_status);\n                        }\n                    }\n                    eprintln!();\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Display diagnostics about rejected/not-found tools\n            if !diagnostics.rejections.is_empty() {\n                eprintln!(\"Detection details:\");\n                for rejection in &diagnostics.rejections {\n                    match &rejection.reason {\n                        guidance::RejectionReason::NotFound => {\n                            eprintln!(\"  • {} - not found in PATH\", rejection.tool_name);\n                        }\n                        guidance::RejectionReason::MissingApiKey { env_var, .. } => {\n                            eprintln!(\"  • {} - missing API key ({})\", rejection.tool_name, env_var);\n                        }\n                        guidance::RejectionReason::IncompatibleVersion { version, missing_feature, .. } => {\n                            let ver = version.as_deref().unwrap_or(\"unknown\");\n                            eprintln!(\"  • {} {} - incompatible: {}\", rejection.tool_name, ver, missing_feature);\n                        }\n                        guidance::RejectionReason::NotExecutable(_) => {\n                            eprintln!(\"  • {} - not executable\", rejection.tool_name);\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n                eprintln!();\n            }\n\n            // Summary\n            let ready_count = tools.iter().filter(|t| t.is_ready()).count();\n            if ready_count > 0 {\n                eprintln!(\"✅ {} tool(s) ready for use\", ready_count);\n                eprintln!(\"   Run 'forge init' to configure\");\n            } else {\n                eprintln!(\"❌ No compatible tools ready\");\n                eprintln!(\"   Install Claude Code, OpenCode, or configure API keys\");\n            }\n\n            ExitCode::SUCCESS\n        }\n        Err(e) => {\n            eprintln!(\"❌ Detection failed: {}\", e);\n            ExitCode::from(1)\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Validate the config file and offer recovery if invalid.\nfn validate_config() -> Result<(), String> {\n    use std::io::{self, Write};\n\n    match ForgeConfig::load_with_error() {\n        Ok(_config) => {\n            info!(\"Configuration validated successfully\");\n            Ok(())\n        }\n        Err(e) => {\n            // Format the error with line/column information\n            eprintln!(\"❌ Configuration Error\");\n            eprintln!();\n\n            let path_str = e.path().map(|p| p.display().to_string())\n                .unwrap_or_else(|| \"~/.forge/config.yaml\".to_string());\n\n            if let (Some(line), Some(col)) = (e.line_number(), e.column_number()) {\n                eprintln!(\"  File: {}\", path_str);\n                eprintln!(\"  Line: {}, Column: {}\", line, col);\n                eprintln!(\"  Error: {}\", e);\n            } else {\n                eprintln!(\"  {}\", e);\n            }\n            eprintln!();\n\n            // Offer recovery options\n            eprintln!(\"Recovery options:\");\n            eprintln!(\"  1) Reset to default configuration (creates backup)\");\n            eprintln!(\"  2) Use defaults without modifying file (temporary)\");\n            eprintln!(\"  3) Exit and fix manually\");\n            eprintln!();\n            eprint!(\"Choose option [1-3]: \");\n            io::stdout().flush().map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;\n\n            let mut choice = String::new();\n            io::stdin().read_line(&mut choice).map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;\n\n            match choice.trim() {\n                \"1\" => {\n                    if let Err(e) = reset_config_to_defaults() {\n                        return Err(format!(\"Failed to reset config: {}\", e));\n                    }\n                    eprintln!(\"✅ Configuration reset to defaults\");\n                    eprintln!(\"   Previous config backed up\");\n                    eprintln!();\n                    Ok(())\n                }\n                \"2\" => {\n                    eprintln!(\"⚠️  Using default configuration (file not modified)\");\n                    eprintln!(\"   Fix the config file manually or delete it to regenerate\");\n                    eprintln!();\n                    Ok(())\n                }\n                \"3\" | \"\" => {\n                    Err(\"Exiting. Please fix the config file and try again.\".to_string())\n                }\n                _ => {\n                    Err(\"Invalid choice. Exiting.\".to_string())\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Reset config file to defaults with backup.\nfn reset_config_to_defaults() -> Result<(), Box<dyn std::error::Error>> {\n    let forge_dir = get_forge_dir();\n    let config_path = forge_dir.join(\"config.yaml\");\n\n    // Create backup\n    if config_path.exists() {\n        let timestamp = chrono::Local::now().format(\"%Y%m%d_%H%M%S\");\n        let backup_path = forge_dir.join(format!(\"config.yaml.backup.{}\", timestamp));\n        std::fs::copy(&config_path, &backup_path)?;\n        info!(\"Created config backup: {}\", backup_path.display());\n    }\n\n    // Generate default config\n    let default_config = r#\"# FORGE Configuration\n# This file was automatically generated after a config error.\n\ndashboard:\n  refresh_interval_ms: 1000\n  max_fps: 60\n  default_layout: overview\n\ntheme:\n  name: default\n\ncost_tracking:\n  enabled: true\n  budget_warning_threshold: 70\n  budget_critical_threshold: 90\n  # monthly_budget_usd: 100.0\n\n# Chat backend configuration (optional)\n# Uncomment and configure if using the chat feature:\n# chat_backend:\n#   command: claude-code\n#   args:\n#     - --headless\n#     - --model\n#     - sonnet\n#   model: sonnet\n\"#;\n\n    std::fs::write(&config_path, default_config)?;\n    info!(\"Reset config to defaults: {}\", config_path.display());\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Handle worker subcommand actions.\nfn handle_worker_action(action: &WorkerAction) -> ExitCode {\n    let writer = match StatusWriter::new(None) {\n        Ok(w) => w,\n        Err(e) => {\n            eprintln!(\"❌ Failed to initialize status writer: {}\", e);\n            return ExitCode::from(1);\n        }\n    };\n\n    match action {\n        WorkerAction::Pause { id } => {\n            if id.to_lowercase() == \"all\" {\n                match writer.pause_all() {\n                    Ok(count) => {\n                        if count == 0 {\n                            eprintln!(\"No workers to pause\");\n                        } else {\n                            eprintln!(\"⏸️  Paused {} worker(s)\", count);\n                        }\n                        ExitCode::SUCCESS\n                    }\n                    Err(e) => {\n                        eprintln!(\"❌ Failed to pause workers: {}\", e);\n                        ExitCode::from(1)\n                    }\n                }\n            } else {\n                match writer.pause_worker(id) {\n                    Ok(()) => {\n                        eprintln!(\"⏸️  Paused worker: {}\", id);\n                        ExitCode::SUCCESS\n                    }\n                    Err(e) => {\n                        eprintln!(\"❌ Failed to pause worker '{}': {}\", id, e);\n                        ExitCode::from(1)\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        WorkerAction::Resume { id } => {\n            if id.to_lowercase() == \"all\" {\n                match writer.resume_all() {\n                    Ok(count) => {\n                        if count == 0 {\n                            eprintln!(\"No workers to resume\");\n                        } else {\n                            eprintln!(\"▶️  Resumed {} worker(s)\", count);\n                        }\n                        ExitCode::SUCCESS\n                    }\n                    Err(e) => {\n                        eprintln!(\"❌ Failed to resume workers: {}\", e);\n                        ExitCode::from(1)\n                    }\n                }\n            } else {\n                match writer.resume_worker(id) {\n                    Ok(()) => {\n                        eprintln!(\"▶️  Resumed worker: {}\", id);\n                        ExitCode::SUCCESS\n                    }\n                    Err(e) => {\n                        eprintln!(\"❌ Failed to resume worker '{}': {}\", id, e);\n                        ExitCode::from(1)\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Handle the `forge validate` command.\nfn handle_validate_command(verbose: bool, fix: bool, skip_backend_test: bool, json: bool) -> ExitCode {\n    info!(\n        \"Handling validate command (verbose={}, fix={}, skip_backend_test={}, json={})\",\n        verbose, fix, skip_backend_test, json\n    );\n\n    let forge_dir = get_forge_dir();\n\n    // Run comprehensive validation\n    let results = validator::validate_comprehensive(&forge_dir, verbose, fix, skip_backend_test);\n\n    // Output results\n    if json {\n        // JSON output\n        match serde_json::to_string_pretty(&results) {\n            Ok(json_output) => {\n                println!(\"{}\", json_output);\n            }\n            Err(e) => {\n                eprintln!(\"❌ Failed to serialize results to JSON: {}\", e);\n                return ExitCode::from(1);\n            }\n        }\n    } else {\n        // Human-readable output\n        print_validation_results(&results, verbose);\n    }\n\n    // Return appropriate exit code\n    if results.passed {\n        ExitCode::SUCCESS\n    } else {\n        ExitCode::from(1)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Print validation results in human-readable format.\nfn print_validation_results(results: // Create client\n        let client = ForgeClient::new(forge_server::client::ClientConfig {\n            server_url,\n            user_id,\n            password,\n        });\n\n        // Subscribe to state updates BEFORE connecting\n        let mut state_rx = client.subscribe();\n\n        // Spawn connection task (client.connect_and_run no longer consumes self)\n        let client_clone = client.clone();\n        let response_tx_clone = response_tx.clone();\n        tokio::spawn(async move {\n            if let Err(e) = client_clone.connect_and_run().await {\n                let _ = response_tx_clone.send(ServerClientMessage::ConnectionError {\n                    message: e.to_string(),\n                });\n            } else {\n                let _ = response_tx_clone.send(ServerClientMessage::Disconnected);\n            }\n        });\n\n        // Task to forward state updates from server to TUI\n        let response_tx_state = response_tx.clone();\n        tokio::spawn(async move {\n            while let Ok(server_msg) = state_rx.recv().await {\n                let tui_msg = match server_msg {\n {"type":"assistant","message":{"id":"msg_20260523060632062d71e54e7b4d76","type":"message","role":"assistant","model":"glm-4.7","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"Now I see the difference. }\n        }\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Send a message to the server.\n    async fn send_message(&self, msg: ClientMessage) {\n        if let Some(write_tx) = self.write_tx.lock().await.as_ref() {\n            let _ = write_tx.send(msg);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Subscribe to state updates.\n    pub fn subscribe(&self) ->
